<p>
「塔」を見物したのはあたかもこの<span class="vocab" onclick="">方法<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>方法</rb><rt>ほうほう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;method; means</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">依らねば<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>依</rb><rt>よ</rt></ruby>らねば&nbsp;without relying on</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">外出<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>外出</rb><rt>がいしゅつ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;excursion; arrive</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">来所<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>来所</rb><rt>らいしょ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;places through which one comes</span></span>なく<span class="vocab" onclick="">去る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>去</rb><rt>さ</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;go; traverse</span></span>「塔」に<span class="vocab" onclick="">着した<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>着</rb><rt>ちゃく</rt></ruby>した&nbsp;arrived (at)</span></span>かまたいかなる<span class="vocab" onclick="">町<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>町</rb><rt>まち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;street; </p>

<p>
倫敦塔の<span class="vocab" onclick="">歴史<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>歴史</rb><rt>れきし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;history</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">英国<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>英国</rb><rt>えいこく</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Britain; </p>

</p>

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">我が<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>我</rb><rt>わ</rt></ruby>が&nbsp;my; one's own</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">前<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>前</rb><rt>まえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;before; prior</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">物<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>物</rb><rt>もの</rt></ruby>&nbsp;things; material; matter</span></span>なしただ<span class="vocab" onclick="">無窮<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無窮</rb><rt>むきゅう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eternity; infinitude</span></span>あり<span class="vocab" onclick="">我<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>我</rb><rt>われ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;I; me; oneself</span></span>は無窮に<span class="vocab" onclick="">忍ぶ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>忍</rb><rt>しの</rt></ruby>ぶ&nbsp;endure</span></span>ものなり。
</p>

<p>
この門を<span class="vocab" onclick="">過ぎん<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>過</rb><rt>す</rt></ruby>ぎん&nbsp;pass through</span></span>とするものはいっさいの<span class="vocab" onclick="">望<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>望</rb><rt>のぞみ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;wishes; desires; hopes</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">捨てよ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>捨</rb><rt>す</rt></ruby>てよ&nbsp;abandon; discard</span></span>。
</p>

<p>
という<span class="vocab" onclick="">句<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>句</rb><rt>く</rt></ruby>&nbsp;words; verses</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">どこぞ<span class="vocabdef">どこぞ&nbsp;somewhere; someplace (vague; undetermined)</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">刻んで<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>刻</rb><rt>きざ</rt></ruby>んで&nbsp;carve; chisel; engrave</span></span>はないかと<span class="vocab" onclick="">思った<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;thought; wondered</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">余<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>余</rb><rt>よ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;I (archaic)</span></span>はこの<span class="vocab" onclick="">時<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>時</rb><rt>とき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;time</span></span>すでに<span class="vocab" onclick="">常態<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>常態</rb><rt>じょうたい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;normalcy</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">失って<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>失</rb><rt>うしな</rt></ruby>って&nbsp;lose; part with</span></span>いる。
</p>

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">空濠<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>空濠</rb><rt>からほり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;dry moat</span></span>にかけてある<span class="vocab" onclick="">石橋<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>石橋</rb><rt>いしばし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;stone bridge</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">渡って行く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>渡</rb><rt>わた</rt></ruby>って<ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;go across; <p>
また<span class="vocab" onclick="">少し<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>少</rb><rt>すこ</rt></ruby>し&nbsp;a little; a bit</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">行く<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>ゆ</rt></ruby>く&nbsp;go; <p>

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">兄<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>兄</rb><rt>あに</rt></ruby>&nbsp;older brother; elder brother</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">優しく<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>優</rb><rt>やさ</rt></ruby>しく&nbsp;gently; softly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">清らかな<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>清</rb><rt>きよ</rt></ruby>らかな&nbsp;clear; pure</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">声<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>声</rb><rt>こえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;voice</span></span>で<span class="vocab" onclick="">膝<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>膝</rb><rt>ひざ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;lap; knees</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">上<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>上</rb><rt>うえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;top of</span></span>なる<span class="vocab" onclick="">書物<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>書物</rb><rt>しょもつ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;book</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">読む<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>読</rb><rt>よ</rt></ruby>む&nbsp;read</span></span>。

<p>
「<span class="vocab" onclick="">我が<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>我</rb><rt>わ</rt></ruby>が&nbsp;my; one's own</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>眼</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">前<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>前</rb><rt>まえ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;before; </p>

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">弟<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>弟</rb><rt>おとうと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;younger brother</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">世に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>世</rb><rt>よ</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;extremely; </p>

<p>
「<span class="vocab" onclick="">朝<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>朝</rb><rt>あさ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;morning</span></span>ならば<span class="vocab" onclick="">夜<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>夜</rb><rt>よる</rt></ruby>&nbsp;evening; night</span></span>の前に死ぬと思え。夜ならば<span class="vocab" onclick="">翌日<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>翌日</rb><rt>あす</rt></ruby>&nbsp;morrow; following day</span></span>ありと<span class="vocab" onclick="">頼む<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頼</rb><rt>たの</rt></ruby>む&nbsp;request; ask for</span></span>な。<span class="vocab" onclick="">覚悟<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>覚悟</rb><rt>かくご</rt></ruby>&nbsp;resolution; readiness; resignation</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">こそ<span class="vocabdef">こそ&nbsp;indeed</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">尊べ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>尊</rb><rt>とうと</rt></ruby>べ&nbsp;value; prize</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">見苦しき<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見苦</rb><rt>みぐる</rt></ruby>しき&nbsp;unsightly; ugly</span></span>死に様ぞ<span class="vocab" onclick="">恥<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>恥</rb><rt>はじ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;shame; disgrace</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">極み<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>極</rb><rt>きわ</rt></ruby>み&nbsp;limit; extreme</span></span>なる……」
</p>

<p>
弟また「アーメン」と云う。その声は<span class="vocab" onclick="">顫えて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>顫</rb><rt>ふる</rt></ruby>えて&nbsp;tremble; shake; quiver</span></span>いる。兄は<span class="vocab" onclick="">静かに<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>静</rb><rt>しず</rt></ruby>かに&nbsp;quietly; calmly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">書<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>書</rb><rt>しょ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;book</span></span>をふせて、かの<span class="vocab" onclick="">小さき<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>小</rb><rt>ちい</rt></ruby>さき&nbsp;small</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">窓<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>窓</rb><rt>まど</rt></ruby>&nbsp;window</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">方<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>方</rb><rt>かた</rt></ruby>&nbsp;direction</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">歩みよりて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>歩</rb><rt>あゆ</rt></ruby>みよりて&nbsp;walk over (to)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">外<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>外</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>&nbsp;outside</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">面<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>面</rb><rt>も</rt></ruby>&nbsp;face; surface</span></span>を見ようとする。窓が高くて<span class="vocab" onclick="">背<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>背</rb><rt>せ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;height; stature</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">足りぬ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>足</rb><rt>た</rt></ruby>りぬ&nbsp;be insufficient; <p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">忽然<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>忽然</rb><rt>こつぜん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;suddenly</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">舞台<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>舞台</rb><rt>ぶたい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;stage; 「<span class="vocab" onclick="">逢う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>逢</rb><rt>あ</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;meet; see</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">事<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>事</rb><rt>こと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;act; action</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">許されて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>許</rb><rt>ゆる</rt></ruby>されて&nbsp;be allowed; be granted</span></span>か」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">女<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>女</rb><rt>おんな</rt></ruby>&nbsp;woman</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">問う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>問</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;ask</span></span>。

<p>
女は<span class="vocab" onclick="">頸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>頸</rb><rt>うなじ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;nape (of the neck)</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">懸けたる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>懸</rb><rt>か</rt></ruby>けたる&nbsp;is hung (on)</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">金<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>金</rb><rt>きん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;gold</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">鎖<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>鎖</rb><rt>くさり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;chain</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">解いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>解</rb><rt>と</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;unfasten</span></span>男に<span class="vocab" onclick="">与えて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>与</rb><rt>あた</rt></ruby>えて&nbsp;give; <p>

<p>
「いかにしても逢う事は<span class="vocab" onclick="">叶わずや<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>叶</rb><rt>かな</rt></ruby>わずや&nbsp;not be granted</span></span>」と女が<span class="vocab" onclick="">尋ねる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>尋</rb><rt>たず</rt></ruby>ねる&nbsp;ask; inquire</span></span>。
</p>

<p>
「<span class="vocab" onclick="">御気の毒なれど<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>御気</rb><rt>ごき</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>毒</rb><rt>どく</rt></ruby>なれど&nbsp;I am sorry</span></span>」と<span class="vocab" onclick="">牢守<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>牢守</rb><rt>ろうもり</rt></ruby>&nbsp;prison guard; jailer</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">云い放つ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>云</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>い<ruby><rb>放</rb><rt>はな</rt></ruby>つ&nbsp;state with finality; assert</span></span>。

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">倫敦塔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>倫敦塔</rb><rt>ロンドンとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;The Tower of London</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">歴史<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>歴史</rb><rt>れきし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;history</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">ボーシャン塔<span class="vocabdef">ボーシャン<ruby><rb>塔</rb><rt>とう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Beauchamp Tower</span></span>の歴史であって、ボーシャン塔の歴史は<span class="vocab" onclick="">悲酸<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>悲酸</rb><rt>ひさん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;tragedy; disaster; misfortune</span></span>の歴史である。<span class="vocab" onclick="">十四世紀<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>十四</rb><rt>じゅうよん</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>世紀</rb><rt>せいき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;fourteenth century</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">後半<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>後半</rb><rt>こうはん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;latter half</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">エドワード三世<span class="vocabdef">エドワード<ruby><rb>三世</rb><rt>さんせい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;Edward III</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">建立<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>建立</rb><rt>こんりゅう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;(act of) building; construction</span></span>にかかるこの<span class="vocab" onclick="">三層塔<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>三層塔</rb><rt>さんそうとう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;three-story tower</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">一階室<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>一階室</rb><rt>いっかいしつ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;first-floor room</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">入る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>入</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;enter</span></span>ものはその入るの<span class="vocab" onclick="">瞬間<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>瞬間</rb><rt>しゅんかん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;instant; </p>

<p>
こんなものを書く人の心の<span class="vocab" onclick="">中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>うち</rt></ruby>&nbsp;inside; within</span></span>はどのようであったろうと<span class="vocab" onclick="">想像して見る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>想像</rb><rt>そうぞう</rt></ruby>して<ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;try to imagine</span></span>。およそ<span class="vocab" onclick="">世の中<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>世</rb><rt>よ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>なか</rt></ruby>&nbsp;the world</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">何<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>何</rb><rt>なに</rt></ruby>&nbsp;what</span></span>が<span class="vocab" onclick="">苦しい<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>苦</rb><rt>くる</rt></ruby>しい&nbsp;painful; have at one's disposal</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">身体<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>身体</rb><rt>からだ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;body; one's person</span></span>は<span class="vocab" onclick="">目<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>目</rb><rt>め</rt></ruby>&nbsp;eyes</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">見えぬ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>えぬ&nbsp;not visible; consequence</span></span>であろう。
</p>

<p>

<p>
と<span class="vocab" onclick="">高調子<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>高調子</rb><rt>たかぢょうし</rt></ruby>&nbsp;in high spirits; with great vigor</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">歌う<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>歌</rb><rt>うた</rt></ruby>う&nbsp;sing</span></span>。シュシュシュと<span class="vocab" onclick="">轆轤<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>轆轤</rb><rt>ろくろ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;trunnion wheel; wield</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">灯影<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>灯影</rb><rt>ほかげ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;flickering flame; dancing firelight</span></span>に刃を<span class="vocab" onclick="">見る<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>見</rb><rt>み</rt></ruby>る&nbsp;look at; </p>

Yow that the beasts do wel behold and se,

May deme with ease wherefore here made they be

Withe borders wherein ……………………………………

4 brothers' names who list to serche the grovnd.

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">気味が悪くなった<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>気味</rb><rt>きみ</rt></ruby>が<ruby><rb>悪</rb><rt>わる</rt></ruby>くなった&nbsp;had become ill at ease; had grown uncomfortable</span></span>から<span class="vocab" onclick="">通り過ぎて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>通</rb><rt>とお</rt></ruby>り<ruby><rb>過</rb><rt>す</rt></ruby>ぎて&nbsp;pass by</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">先<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>先</rb><rt>さき</rt></ruby>&nbsp;ahead</span></span>へ<span class="vocab" onclick="">抜ける<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>抜</rb><rt>ぬ</rt></ruby>ける&nbsp;pass through</span></span>。<span class="vocab" onclick="">銃眼<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>銃眼</rb><rt>じゅうがん</rt></ruby>&nbsp;embrasure; <p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">無我夢中に<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>無我夢中</rb><rt>むがむちゅう</rt></ruby>に&nbsp;lost in one's thoughts; in a dream</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">宿<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>宿</rb><rt>やど</rt></ruby>&nbsp;lodgings</span></span>に<span class="vocab" onclick="">着いて<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>着</rb><rt>つ</rt></ruby>いて&nbsp;reach; <p>
それからは<span class="vocab" onclick="">人<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>人</rb><rt>ひと</rt></ruby>&nbsp;people; others</span></span>と倫敦塔の話しをしない事にきめた。また<span class="vocab" onclick="">再び<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>再</rb><rt>ふたた</rt></ruby>び&nbsp;again; once more; a second time</span></span>見物に行かない事にきめた。
</p>

</p>

<SectionBreak
	studyguide='/london/studyguide19'
	audio={''}
	num={19}
/>

The axe was sharp, and heavy as lead,

As it touched the neck, off went the head!

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whir―whir―whir―whir!

Queen Anne laid her white throat upon the block,

Quietly waiting the fatal shock;

The axe it severed it right in twain,

And so quick―so true―that she felt no pain.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whir―whir―whir―whir!

Salisbury's countess, she would not die

As a proud dame should―decorously.

Lifting my axe, I split her skull,

And the edge since then has been notched and dull.

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whir―whir―whir―whir!

Queen Catherine Howard gave me a fee, ―

A chain of gold―to die easily:

And her costly present she did not rue,

For I touched her head, and away it flew!

&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Whir―whir―whir―whir!

<p>
この<span class="vocab" onclick="">全章<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>全章</rb><rt>ぜんしょう</rt></ruby>&nbsp;entire composition; complete passage</span></span>を<span class="vocab" onclick="">訳そう<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>訳</rb><rt>やく</rt></ruby>そう&nbsp;translate</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">と思った<span class="vocabdef">と<ruby><rb>思</rb><rt>おも</rt></ruby>った&nbsp;thought to ...</span></span>がとうてい思うように<span class="vocab" onclick="">行かない<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>行</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>かない&nbsp;not go; not proceed</span></span>し、かつ<span class="vocab" onclick="">余り<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>余</rb><rt>あま</rt></ruby>り&nbsp;too much</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">長過ぎる<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>長過</rb><rt>ながす</rt></ruby>ぎる&nbsp;be too long; be too lengthy</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">恐れ<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>恐</rb><rt>おそ</rt></ruby>れ&nbsp;fear concern</span></span>があるからやめにした。
</p>

<p>
<span class="vocab" onclick="">二王子<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>二王子</rb><rt>におうじ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;two princes</span></span><span class="vocab" onclick="">幽閉<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>幽閉</rb><rt>ゆうへい</rt></ruby>&nbsp;confinement; comment briefly on</span></span>いささか<span class="vocab" onclick="">感謝<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>感謝</rb><rt>かんしゃ</rt></ruby>&nbsp;gratitude</span></span>の<span class="vocab" onclick="">意<span class="vocabdef"><ruby><rb>意</rb><rt>い</rt></ruby>&nbsp;feelings;
